<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 350);
	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 350);
	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>

<script>
function h_nav(){
	var oDiv=document.getElementById('tab');
	var aBtn=oDiv.getElementsByTagName('li');
	var oSpan=document.getElementById('main');
	var aSpan=oSpan.getElementsByTagName('section');
	var i=0;
	for(i=0;i<aBtn.length;i++)
	{
		aBtn[i].index=i;
		aBtn[i].onclick=function ()
		{
			for(i=0;i<aBtn.length;i++)
			{
				aBtn[i].className='';
				aSpan[i].className='';
				
			}
			this.className='show';
			aSpan[this.index].className='ls_show';
		};
	}
}h_nav();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function morelist(tag,url){
	i=0;
	$(".cat_"+tag).each(function(){
		if ($(this).css('display')=='none'){
			$(this).show();
			i++;
		}
		if(i>=5){return false;}
	});
	if(i==0){
		window.location.href=url;
	}
	if($(".cat_"+tag+":hidden").length<=0){
		if(!url){
			$(".more_"+tag).hide();
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){

	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>

<script>
function _GET(varName){
	var arrayTemp = new Array(); 
	url = location.search.substr(1);
	if(url.length > 0) {
		ar = url.split(/[&=]/);
		for(i=0;i<ar.length;i+=2) {
			if (decodeURIComponent(ar[i]) == varName){
				arrayTemp.push(decodeURIComponent(ar[i+1]));
			}
		}
	}
	if (arrayTemp.length<=0){
		return false;
	}else if(arrayTemp.length<=1){
		return arrayTemp[0];
	}else{
		return arrayTemp;//return String(arrayTemp);
	}
}

                                    function oRandom(){								
                                            var jctp_main = document.getElementById("marqueebox0");
                                            var j = 0;
                                            var div_jctp = jctp_main.getElementsByTagName("li");
                                            var divData = [];

                                                divData.push(div_jctp[j]);

                                        function startmarquee_weibo(lh,speed,delay,index){ 
                                            var t; 
                                            var p=false; 
                                            var o=document.getElementById("marqueebox"+index); 
                                            var oid=document.getElementById("marquee"); 
                                            o.innerHTML+=o.innerHTML; 
                                            o.onmouseover=function(){p=true} 
                                            o.onmouseout=function(){p=false} 
                                            o.scrollTop = 0; 
                                            function start(){ 
                                               t=setInterval(scrolling,speed); 
                                               if(!p) o.scrollTop += 1; 
                                            } 
                                            function scrolling()
                                            { 
                                               if(o.scrollTop%lh!=0)
                                               { 
                                                o.scrollTop += 1; 
                                                if(o.scrollTop==o.scrollHeight/2)
                                                    o.scrollTop = 0; 
                                                   }
                                                   else{ 
                                                    clearInterval(t); 
                                                    setTimeout(start,delay); 
                                                   } ;			 
                                            } 
                                            setTimeout(start,delay); 
                                        }

                    <script type="text/javascript">
                        function h_nav()
                            {
                                var oDiv=document.getElementById('more_num');
                                var aBtn=oDiv.getElementsByTagName('span');
                                var oSpan=document.getElementById('more_main');
                                var aSpan=oSpan.getElementsByTagName('ul');
                                var i=0;
                                for(i=0;i<aBtn.length;i++)
                                {
                                    aBtn[i].index=i;
                                    aBtn[i].onmouseover=function ()
                                    {
                                        for(i=0;i<aBtn.length;i++)
                                        {
                                            aBtn[i].className='';
                                            aSpan[i].className='';
                                            
                                        }
                                        this.className='num_show';
                                        aSpan[this.index].className='cent_show';
                                    };
                                }
                            }h_nav();

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 350);
	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>

        (function() {
            var speed = 80;
            var tab = document.getElementById("art_gd");
            var tab1 = document.getElementById("gdxw");
            var tab2 = document.getElementById("gdxw2");

                    tab.scrollTop++;

            tab.onmouseover = function() {
                clearInterval(gundong)

            tab.onmouseout = function() {
                gundong = setInterval(Marquee, speed)

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 350);
	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>

        (function() {
            var speed = 80;
            var tab = document.getElementById("art_gd");
            var tab1 = document.getElementById("gdxw");
            var tab2 = document.getElementById("gdxw2");
            tab2.innerHTML = tab1.innerHTML;
            function Marquee() {
                if (tab2.offsetHeight - tab.scrollTop <= 0) tab.scrollTop -= tab2.offsetHeight;
                else {
                    tab.scrollTop++;
                }
            }
            var gundong = setInterval(Marquee, speed);
            tab.onmouseover = function() {
                clearInterval(gundong)
            };
            tab.onmouseout = function() {
                gundong = setInterval(Marquee, speed)
            };
        })();

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 350);
	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        (function() {
            var speed = 80;
            var tab = document.getElementById("art_gd");
            var tab1 = document.getElementById("gdxw");
            var tab2 = document.getElementById("gdxw2");
            tab2.innerHTML = tab1.innerHTML;
            function Marquee() {
                if (tab2.offsetHeight - tab.scrollTop <= 0) tab.scrollTop -= tab2.offsetHeight;
                else {
                    tab.scrollTop++;
                }
            }
            var gundong = setInterval(Marquee, speed);
            tab.onmouseover = function() {
                clearInterval(gundong)
            };
            tab.onmouseout = function() {
                gundong = setInterval(Marquee, speed)
            };
        })();
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
(function(){
	var $backToTopTxt = "",  
	$backToTopEle = $('<div class="backToTop"></div>').appendTo($("body"))
		.text($backToTopTxt).attr("title", $backToTopTxt).click(function(){
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 350);
	}), 
	$backToTopFun = function(){
		var st = $(document).scrollTop(), winh = $(window).height();
		(st > 800)? $backToTopEle.show(): $backToTopEle.hide();
		
		//(st > 800)? fnav.show(): fnav.hide();
		//IE6ä¸çå®ä½
		if(!window.XMLHttpRequest){
			$backToTopEle.css("top", st + winh - 280);
		}
	};
	$(window).bind("scroll", $backToTopFun);
	$(function(){ $backToTopFun(); });
})();
});
</script>
